        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





After looking at 



<span class="line"><!---->After looking at <!----></span>





issue 1310461



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1310461" title="Security: chrome.downloads.download could be abused to steal user's environment variables like secrets, tokens or keys on windows."><!---->issue 1310461<!----></a>





 and



<span class="line"><!----> and<!----></span>





 the `chrome.downloads` API, I found `chrome.downloads.onDeterminingFilename`[1] which states that "During the filename determination process, extensions will be given the opportunity to override the target DownloadItem.filename". Well, it turns out that this can be used to bypass the fix for 



<span class="line"><!----> the `chrome.downloads` API, I found `chrome.downloads.onDeterminingFilename`[1] which states that "During the filename determination process, extensions will be given the opportunity to override the target DownloadItem.filename". Well, it turns out that this can be used to bypass the fix for <!----></span>





issue 1310461



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1310461" title="Security: chrome.downloads.download could be abused to steal user's environment variables like secrets, tokens or keys on windows."><!---->issue 1310461<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://developer.chrome.com/docs/extensions/reference/downloads/#event-onDeterminingFilename



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://developer.chrome.com/docs/extensions/reference/downloads/#event-onDeterminingFilename"><!---->https://developer.chrome.com/docs/extensions/reference/downloads/#event-onDeterminingFilename<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

Yes, I can confirm that the CL fixes the issue, but it seems to have only landed in chrome 105, on chrome 104 it is still reproducible. However, when playing around with the fix, I noticed that there is still a way to leak environment variables. The file extension for a download is automatically generated from the URL path when there is no `filename` specified and by specifying a download URL like `



<span class="line"><!---->Yes, I can confirm that the CL fixes the issue, but it seems to have only landed in chrome 105, on chrome 104 it is still reproducible. However, when playing around with the fix, I noticed that there is still a way to leak environment variables. The file extension for a download is automatically generated from the URL path when there is no `filename` specified and by specifying a download URL like `<!----></span>





https://example.com/test.%USERNAME%`

,



<span class="line"><!---->,<!----></span>

<br>



<br>





Fix an issue extensions can be used to expose env variables



<span class="line"><!---->Fix an issue extensions can be used to expose env variables<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





On windows save file dialog, the file extension type can also be used



<span class="line"><!---->On windows save file dialog, the file extension type can also be used<!----></span>



<br>





to expose env variables. The extension is passed separately from the



<span class="line"><!---->to expose env variables. The extension is passed separately from the<!----></span>



<br>





file name to be saved. This CL sanitizes the extension before it is



<span class="line"><!---->file name to be saved. This CL sanitizes the extension before it is<!----></span>



<br>





being used. The CL also removes unused AppendExtensionIfNeeded().



<span class="line"><!---->being used. The CL also removes unused AppendExtensionIfNeeded().<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
